1A
(CHAPTER 252) MUNICIPAL COUNCILS ORDINANCE
Order
BY virtue of the powers vested in me under Sections 2 and 5 of Municipal Councils Ordinance (Chapter 252) and Section 27F
of Local Authorities Elections Ordinance (Chapter 262) to be read with section 18 of Interpretation Ordinance (Chapter 2), I
Faiszer Musthapha, Minister of Provincial Councils and Local Government, do by this order, amend the order published in
the Gazette Extraordinary No. 329/8 of 10th August, 1978 relating to the Colombo Municipal Council as follows :
1. By the substitution for paragraph (4) thereof, of the following paragraph ;
"(4) Determine that the Colombo Municipal Council shall consist of such number of members to be elected in terms of
following i, ii and iii sub paragraphs.
i. Sixty six members to be elected under paragraph (a) of subsection (1) of section 5 of the Municipal Councils
Ordinance (Chapter 252) ;
ii. Maximum of nineteen members to be retained under paragraph (b) of subsection (1) of section 5 of the Municipal
Councils Ordinance (Chapter 252) ;
iii. Twenty eight female members to be elected under sub section (3) of section 27F of Local Authorities Elections
Ordinance (Chapter 262)"
This order shall come into operation on the 01st day of July 2017.
F
AISZER MUSTHAPHA,
Minister of Provincial Councils and Local Government.
Colombo,
07th of April 2017.

(CHAPTER 252) MUNICIPAL COUNCILS ORDINANCE
Order
BY virtue of the powers vested in me under sections 2 and 5 of Municipal Councils Ordinance (Chapter 252) and section 27F
of Local Authorities Elections Ordinance (Chapter 262) to be read with section 18 of Interpretation Ordinance (Chapter 2), I
Faiszer Musthapha, Minister of Provincial Councils and Local Government, do by this order, amend the order published in
the Gazette Extraordinary No. 329/8 of 10th August, 1978 relating to the Dehiwala-Mt. Lavinia Municipal Council  as
follows:
1. By the substitution for paragraph (4) thereof, of the following paragraph ;
"(4) Determine that the  Dehiwala-Mt. Lavinia Municipal Council shall consist of such number of members to be
elected in terms of following i, ii and iii sub paragraphs.
i. Twenty nine members to be elected under paragraph (a) of subsection (1) of section 5 of the Municipal Councils
Ordinance (Chapter 252) ;
ii. Maximum of eight members to be retained under paragraph (b) of subsection (1) of section 5 of the Municipal
Councils Ordinance (Chapter 252) ;
iii. Twelve female members to be elected under sub section (3) of section 27F of Local Authorities Elections Ordinance
(Chapter 262)"
This order shall come into operation on the 01st day of July 2017.
F
AISZER MUSTHAPHA,
Minister of Provincial Councils and Local Government.
Colombo,
07th of April 2017.

PRADESHIYA SABHA ACT, No. 15 OF 1987
Order
BY virtue of the powers vested in me under sections 1 and 6 of  Pradeshiya Sabha Act and section 27F  of Local Authorities
Elections Ordinance (Chapter 262) to be read with section 18 of Interpretation Ordinance (Chapter 2), I Faiszer Musthapha,
Minister of Provincial Councils and Local Government, do by this order, amend the order published in the Gazette Extraordinary
No. 453/5 of  12th May, 1987 relating to the Homagama Pradeshiya Sabha as follows:
1. By the substitution for paragraph (4) thereof, of the following paragraph ;
"(4) Determine that the Homagama Pradeshiya Sabha shall consist of such number of members to be elected in terms
of following i, ii and iii sub paragraphs.
i. Twenty eight members to be elected under paragraph (a) of subsection  (1) of section 4 of the Pradeshiya Sabha
Act, No. 15 of 1987 ;
ii. Maximum of eight  members to be retained under paragraph (b) of subsection (1) of section 4 of the Pradeshiya
Sabha Act, No. 15 of 1987 ;
iii. Twelve female members to be elected under sub section (3) of section 27F of Local Authorities Elections Ordinance
(Chapter 262)"
This order shall come into operation on the 01st day of July 2017.
F
AISZER MUSTHAPHA,
Minister of Provincial Councils and Local Government.
Colombo,
07th of April 2017.

CHAPTER  (255)  URBAN  COUNCILS  ORDINANCE
Order
BY virtue of the powers vested in me under sections 2 and 5 of Urban Councils Ordinance (Chapter 255) and Section 27F of
Local Authorities Elections Ordinance (Chapter 262) to be read with Section 18 of Interpretation Ordinance (Chapter 2), I
Faiszer Musthapha, Minister of Provincial Councils and Local Government, do by this order, amend the order published in

 (i) Nineteen members to be elected under paragraph (a) of subsection (1) of Section 4 of the Pradeshiya Sabha Act, 
No. 15 of 1987;
 (ii) Maximum of Five members to be retained under paragraph (b) of subsection (1) of Section 4 of the Pradeshiya 
Sabha Act, No. 15 of 1987;
 (iii) Eight Female members to be elected under subsection (3) of Section 27F of Local Authorities Elections Ordinance 
(Chapter 262)”
This order shall come into operation on the 01st day of July, 2017.
 
 
Faiszer Musthapha,
 Minister of Provincial Councils and Local Government.
Colombo,
07th April, 2017.

(Chapter 262)”
This order shall come into operation on the 01st day of July, 2017.
 
 
Faiszer Musthapha,
 Minister of Provincial Councils and Local Government.
Colombo,
07th April, 2017.

order

No. 453/28 of 12th May, 1987 relating to the Mawanella pradeshiya sabha as follows:

“(4) Determine that the Mawanella pradeshiya sabha shall consist of such number of members to be elected in 
terms of following i, ii and iii sub paragraphs.
